\u003ccode\u003eTabItem\u003c/code\u003e with \u003ccode\u003eTabs\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026lt;Tabs labels={[\u0026quot;Content\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;CLI\u0026quot;]}\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;TabItem\u0026gt;\nIn your config v3 project, head to the `/metadata/databases/databases.yaml` file and add the database configuration as below.\n\n```bash showLineNumbers\n- name: \u0026lt;db_name\u0026gt;\n  kind: postgres\n  configuration:\n    connection_info:\n      database_url:\n        from_env: \u0026lt;DB_URL_ENV_VAR\u0026gt;\n    pool_settings:\n      idle_timeout: 180\n      max_connections: 50\n      retries: 1\n  tables: []\n  functions: []\n```\n\nApply the Metadata by running:\n\n```bash\nhasura metadata apply\n```\n\nIf you've spun up the Hasura Engine with Docker, you can access the Hasura Console by accessing it in a browser at the URL of your Hasura Engine instance, usually http://localhost:8080.\n\n\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;note\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nTo access the Hasura Console via the URL the HASURA_GRAPHQL_ENABLE_CONSOLE environment variable or the `--enable-console` flag must be set to true.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;/TabItem\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;TabItem\u0026gt;\nAlternatively, you can create read replicas using the Neon API or Neon CLI.\n\n```bash\ncurl --request POST \\\n     --url https://console.neon.tech/api/v2/projects/late-bar-27572981/endpoints \\\n     --header 'Accept: application/json' \\\n     --header \u0026quot;Authorization: Bearer $NEON_API_KEY\u0026quot; \\\n     --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n     --data '\n{\n  \u0026quot;endpoint\u0026quot;: {\n    \u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;read_only\u0026quot;,\n    \u0026quot;branch_id\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;br-young-fire-15282225\u0026quot;\n  }\n}\n' | jq\n```\n\n\u0026lt;/TabItem\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;/Tabs\u0026gt;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u0026lt;Tabs labels={\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e[\u003c/span\u003e\"Content\", \"CLI\"\u003cspan 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTo improve the documentation readability, one can leverage an Admonition custom component. Just wrap your piece of text with \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;Admonition\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\u003c/code\u003e and pass the type.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThere are 6 types of Admonition: \u003ccode\u003enote\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eimportant\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003etip\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003einfo\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ewarning\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ecomingSoon\u003c/code\u003e; the default is \u003ccode\u003enote\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou may also specify an optional title with prop \u003ccode\u003etitle\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;note\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nHighlights information that users should take into account, even when skimming.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;important\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nCrucial information necessary for users to succeed.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;tip\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nOptional information to help a user be more successful.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;info\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nInformation that helps users understand the things better.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;warning\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nCritical content demanding immediate user attention due to potential risks.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;Admonition type=\u0026quot;comingSoon\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\nInformation about features that are coming soon.\n\u0026lt;/Admonition\u0026gt;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u0026lt;\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-e\"\u003etype\u003c/span\u003e=\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003enote\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\nHighlights information that users should take into account, even when skimming.\n\u0026lt;/\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-e\"\u003etype\u003c/span\u003e=\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eimportant\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\nCrucial information necessary for users to succeed.\n\u0026lt;/\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-e\"\u003etype\u003c/span\u003e=\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003etip\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\nOptional information to help a user be more successful.\n\u0026lt;/\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\n\n\u0026lt;\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003eAdmonition\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-e\"\u003etype\u003c/span\u003e=\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003einfo\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u0026gt;\nInformation that helps users understand the things better.\n\u0026lt;/\u003cspan '2026-03-23T12:18:17.899Z'","---","","# Docs","","Welcome to Neon docs! This folder contains the source code of the [Neon docs](/docs/).","","## Basic information","","1. Every single Markdown file in this folder will be turned into a docs page.","2. Folder and file names should follow kebab-case.","3. `slug` is generated based on the folder structure and file names inside this folder. In order to see page `slug`, you can [start](../../README.md#run-the-website) and build the project with `npm run build` command that will display all generated pages.","4. Page `path` is generated by combining [`DOCS_BASE_PATH`](../../src/constants/docs.js) and page `slug`.","5. There is no need to add `h1` to the page since it will be displayed automatically with the value from `title` field.","","## Fields","","Right now Markdown files accept the following fields:","","1. `title` — title of the page (required)","2. `subTitle` — subtitle of the page.","3. `tag` — tag for the page. It can be one of the following: `new`, `beta`, `coming soon`, `deprecated`, or you can use your own tag. Don't forget to add it to the `navigation.yaml` file as well.","4. `redirectFrom` — array of strings with paths to redirect from to the page, should start and end with a slash, for example `/docs/old-path/`","5. `isDraft` — flag that says the page is not ready yet. It won't appear in production but will appear in the development mode.","6. `enableTableOfContents` — flag that turns on the display of the outline for the page. The outline gets built out of second and third-level headings ([`h2`, `h3`]), thus appears as two-level nested max.","7. `ogImage` - the social preview image of the page.","","\u003e ⚠️ Please note that the project won't build if at least one of the Markdown files is missing a required field.","","## Navigation","","Navigation data is stored in the [navigation.yaml](./navigation.yaml) file.","","### Navigation Structure","","The navigation system is a unified structure where:","","- **Top-level items** appear in the header navigation","- **Child items** appear in the left sidebar","","This creates a seamless navigation experience where users select a main category from the header and see its detailed structure in the sidebar.","","### Top Navigation Structure","","Each top-level navigation item has the following structure:","","```yaml","- nav: Get started # Navigation label (displayed in header)","  slug: introduction # URL slug for the section","  title: Neon Docs # Page title","  icon: home # Icon identifier","  subnav: # Sub-navigation items for header dropdowns","    - title: Neon platform","      slug: manage/platform","      icon: settings","      items: # Sidebar navigation items","        ...","```","","**Important**: Top-level items can contain either:","","- **`subnav`**: Sub-navigation items that appear as header dropdowns","- **`items`**: Navigation items that appear in the sidebar","","### Sidebar Navigation Structure","","The sidebar navigation supports multiple levels:","","```yaml","  ...","  items: # Sidebar navigation items","    - section: Features # Section header","      icon: features","      slug: guides/neon-features","      items: # Section items","        - title: Serverless","          slug: introduction/serverless","        - title: Autoscaling","          slug: introduction/autoscaling","          items: # Section subitems","            - title: Introduction","              slug: introduction/autoscaling","            - title: Architecture","              slug: introduction/autoscaling-architecture","```","","### How to add a new top navigation category","","To add a new top-level navigation category, add a new item to the top level array with keys `nav`, `slug`, `title`, `icon`, and optionally `items` or `subnav`.","","```diff","+- nav: New Category","+  slug: new-category","+  title: New Category Title","+  icon: new-icon","+  subnav:","+    ...","```","","### How to add a new section","","To add a new section within a navigation category, add a new item with keys `section`, `icon`, and `items`.","","```diff","  ...","  items:","+   - section: Architecture","+     icon: architecture","+     items:","+       ...","```","","### How to add a new page","","To add a new page, add a new item with keys `title` and `slug` under the appropriate section or navigation level.","","```diff","  ...","  items:","+   - title: Overview","+     slug: introduction/architecture-overview","```","","### Navigation Properties","","- `nav`: The label displayed in the top navigation header","- `slug`: The URL path for the page/section","- `title`: The display title for the page/section","- `icon`: Icon identifier for visual representation","- `section`: Section header for grouping related items","- `items`: Array of navigation items","- `subnav`: Sub-navigation items for the sidebar","- `tag`: Optional tag (for example, \"new\", \"beta\") displayed next to the title","","### Important Notes","","- `title` in the sidebar may differ from `title` in the Markdown file","- `slug` should always match the page's slug","- The navigation supports unlimited nesting levels for complex documentation structures","- Icons are referenced by name and should match available icon components","- Tags like \"new\" or \"beta\" are automatically displayed with special styling","","## Code blocks","","All available languages for code blocks can be found [here](https://shiki.matsu.io/languages).","","You can use fenced code blocks with three backticks (```) on the lines before and after the code block. And display code with options","","- enable highlighting single lines, multiple lines, and ranges of code lines","","  Examples:","  - Single line highlight","","    ````md","    ```c++ {1}","    #include \u003ciostream\u003e","","    int main() {","        std::cout \u003c\u003c \"Hello World\";","        return 0;","    }","    ```","    ````","","  - Multiple lines","","    ````md","    ```c++ {1,2,5}","    #include \u003ciostream\u003e","","    int main() {","        std::cout \u003c\u003c \"Hello World\";","        return 0;","    }","    ```","    ````","","  - Range of code lines","","    ````md","    ```c++ {1-3,5}","    #include \u003ciostream\u003e","","    int main() {","        std::cout \u003c\u003c \"Hello World\";","        return 0;","    }","    ```","    ````","","- use `[!code highlight]` to highlight a line.","","  ```ts","  export function foo() {","    console.log('Highlighted'); // [!code highlight]","  }","  ```","","- use `[!code word:xxx]` to highlight a word.","","  ```ts","  export function foo() {","    // [!code word:Hello]","    const msg = 'Hello World';","    console.log(msg);","  }","  ```","","- use `[!code --]` and `[!code ++]` to highlight a code diff.","","  ```ts","  export function foo() {","    const msg = 'Hello Word'; // [!code --]","    const msg = 'Hello World'; // [!code ++]","  }","  ```","","- `showLineNumbers` - flag to show on the line numbers in the code block.","","  Example:","","  ````md","  ```c++ showLineNumbers","  #include \u003ciostream\u003e","","  int main() {","      std::cout \u003c\u003c \"Hello World\";","      return 0;","  }","  ```","  ````","","- `shouldWrap` - flag to enable code wrapping in the code block.","","  Example:","","  ````md","  ```powershell shouldWrap","  powershell -Command \"Start-Process -FilePath powershell -Verb RunAs -ArgumentList '-NoProfile','-InputFormat None','-ExecutionPolicy Bypass','-Command \"\"iex (iwr -UseBasicParsing https://cli.configu.com/install.ps1)\"\"'\"","  ```","  ````","","- `filename=\"...\"` - add a filename label above the code block.","","  Examples:","","  ````md","  ```jsx filename=\"src/App.jsx\"","  export default function App() {","    return \u003cdiv\u003eHello\u003c/div\u003e;","  }","  ```","  ````","","  You can combine it with line highlighting and other flags:","","  ````md","  ```jsx filename=\"src/App.jsx\" {2} showLineNumbers shouldWrap","  export default function App() {","    return \u003cdiv\u003eHello\u003c/div\u003e;","  }","  ```","  ````","","## Code Tabs","","To display code tabs, wrap all pieces of code with `\u003cCodeTabs\u003e\u003c/CodeTabs\u003e` and write labels of code tabs in order:","","````md","\u003cCodeTabs labels={[\"Shell\", \"C++\", \"C#\", \"Java\"]}\u003e","","```bash {2-4}","#!/bin/bash","STR=\"Hello World!\"","echo $STR","```","","```c++","#include \u003ciostream\u003e","","int main() {","    std::cout \u003c\u003c \"Hello World\";","    return 0;","}","```","","```csharp","namespace HelloWorld","{","    class Hello {","        static void Main(string[] args)","        {","            System.Console.WriteLine(\"Hello World\");","        }","    }","}","```","","```java","import java.io.*;","","class GFG {","    public static void main (String[] args) {","       System.out.println(\"Hello World\");","    }","}","```","","\u003c/CodeTabs\u003e","````","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExamples\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Code tabs example](images/code-tabs-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## External Code","","The `ExternalCode` component allows embedding code content from external sources with syntax highlighting.","","### Usage","","```markdown","\u003cExternalCode","  url=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/neondatabase/neon/main/README.md\"","/\u003e","```","","### Props","","| Prop            | Type    | Default    | Description                                                   |","| --------------- | ------- | ---------- | ------------------------------------------------------------- |","| url             | string  | (required) | URL to the raw file                                           |","| language        | string  | (optional) | Language for syntax highlighting (defaults to file extension) |","| shouldWrap      | boolean | false      | Enables code wrapping in the code block                       |","| showLineNumbers | boolean | false      | Shows line numbers in the code block                          |","| className       | string  | ''         | Additional CSS classes to apply to the component              |","","### Best Practices","","1. Always use raw URLs from the GitHub repository (for example, `https://raw.githubusercontent.com/...`).","2. Use the `language` prop when the file extension doesn't match the actual content type.","","## Tabs","","To display the tabs with content as image, video, code block, .etc, wrap the `TabItem` with `Tabs`","","````md","\u003cTabs labels={[\"Content\", \"CLI\"]}\u003e","","\u003cTabItem\u003e","In your config v3 project, head to the `/metadata/databases/databases.yaml` file and add the database configuration as below.","","```bash showLineNumbers","- name: \u003cdb_name\u003e","  kind: postgres","  configuration:","    connection_info:","      database_url:","        from_env: \u003cDB_URL_ENV_VAR\u003e","    pool_settings:","      idle_timeout: 180","      max_connections: 50","      retries: 1","  tables: []","  functions: []","```","","Apply the Metadata by running:","","```bash","hasura metadata apply","```","","If you've spun up the Hasura Engine with Docker, you can access the Hasura Console by accessing it in a browser at the URL of your Hasura Engine instance, usually http://localhost:8080.","","\u003cAdmonition type=\"note\"\u003e","To access the Hasura Console via the URL the HASURA_GRAPHQL_ENABLE_CONSOLE environment variable or the `--enable-console` flag must be set to true.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","","\u003c/TabItem\u003e","","\u003cTabItem\u003e","Alternatively, you can create read replicas using the Neon API or Neon CLI.","","```bash","curl --request POST \\","     --url https://console.neon.tech/api/v2/projects/late-bar-27572981/endpoints \\","     --header 'Accept: application/json' \\","     --header \"Authorization: Bearer $NEON_API_KEY\" \\","     --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \\","     --data '","{","  \"endpoint\": {","    \"type\": \"read_only\",","    \"branch_id\": \"br-young-fire-15282225\"","  }","}","' | jq","```","","\u003c/TabItem\u003e","","\u003c/Tabs\u003e","````","","## Admonition","","To improve the documentation readability, one can leverage an Admonition custom component. Just wrap your piece of text with `\u003cAdmonition\u003e\u003c/Admonition\u003e` and pass the type.","","There are 6 types of Admonition: `note`, `important`, `tip`, `info`, `warning`, `comingSoon`; the default is `note`.","","You may also specify an optional title with prop `title`.","","Example:","","```md","\u003cAdmonition type=\"note\"\u003e","Highlights information that users should take into account, even when skimming.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","","\u003cAdmonition type=\"important\"\u003e","Crucial information necessary for users to succeed.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","","\u003cAdmonition type=\"tip\"\u003e","Optional information to help a user be more successful.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","","\u003cAdmonition type=\"info\"\u003e","Information that helps users understand the things better.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","","\u003cAdmonition type=\"warning\"\u003e","Critical content demanding immediate user attention due to potential risks.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","","\u003cAdmonition type=\"comingSoon\"\u003e","Information about features that are coming soon.","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","```","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExamples\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Admonition example](images/admonition-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## CTA","","This is a simple block with title, description text and one CTA button that accomplish certain actions.","","```md","\u003cCTA /\u003e","```","","Check the example for default data of CTA block","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExample\u003c/summary\u003e","","![CTA example](images/cta-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","To change text in CTA block, you can pass to the component props `title`, `description`, `buttonText`, `buttonUrl`:","","```md","\u003cCTA title=\"Try it on Neon!\" description=\"Neon is Serverless Postgres built for the cloud. Explore Postgres features and functions in our user-friendly SQL Editor. Sign up for a free account to get started.\" buttonText=\"Sign Up\" buttonUrl=\"https://console.neon.tech/signup\" /\u003e","```","","## Steps","","To display numbered steps, wrap the content with `Steps` component.  ","Steps will be splitted by `h2` headings.","","```md","\u003cSteps\u003e","","## Step 1: Create the Initial Schema","","First, create a new database called `people` on the `main` branch and add some sample data to it.","","## Step 2: Create a development branch","","Create a new development branch off of `main`. This branch will be an exact, isolated copy of `main`.","","\u003c/Steps\u003e","```","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExample\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Steps example](images/steps-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## Two Column Layout","","The `TwoColumnLayout` component creates a two-column layout for tutorial pages and reference documentation. Use `TwoColumnLayout.Step` for numbered tutorial steps or `TwoColumnLayout.Item` for default items. Nested content blocks should be wrapped with `TwoColumnLayout.Block`.","","\u003e **Note:** Pages using `TwoColumnLayout` should include `layout: wide` prop to hide the right sidebar (Table of Contents) and provide more space for the two-column layout.","","Check [Neon Auth with Next.js](https://neon.com/docs/auth/quick-start/nextjs-api-only) and [Neon TypeScript SDK](https://neon.com/docs/reference/javascript-sdk) for usage examples.","","````md","\u003cTwoColumnLayout\u003e","","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Step title=\"Install dependencies\"\u003e","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","","Install the required packages for your project.","","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Block label=\"Terminal\"\u003e","","```bash","npm install @neondatabase/neon-js","```","","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Step\u003e","","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Item title=\"Sign in with email\" method=\"auth.signIn.email()\" id=\"signin-email\"\u003e","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","","Authenticate a user with their email and password.","","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","","```typescript","await client.auth.signIn.email({","  email: 'user@example.com',","  password: 'password123',","});","```","","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Block\u003e","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Item\u003e","","\u003cTwoColumnLayout.Footer\u003e","\u003cAdmonition type=\"note\"\u003e","Additional information that spans both columns","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout.Footer\u003e","","\u003c/TwoColumnLayout\u003e","````","","**Components:**","","- `TwoColumnLayout.Step` - Numbered step with `title` prop (for tutorials)","- `TwoColumnLayout.Item` - Default item with `title`, `method`, and `id` prop","- `TwoColumnLayout.Block` - Nested content block with optional `label` prop","- `TwoColumnLayout.Footer` - Full-width content at the bottom of a step","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExamples\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Two Column Layout example](images/two-column-layout-example.jpg)","","Example with steps:","","![Two Column Layout example](images/two-column-layout-steps-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## Feature List","","To display a list of features, use the `FeatureList` component.","Features will be splitted by `h2` and `h3` headings.","","```md","\u003cFeatureList\u003e","","### Agent creates an app","","A vibe coder imagines an app. Your agent builds it, full-stack.","","### Gets a working database instantly, with no friction","","Neon provisions the database behind the scenes via API.","","\u003c/FeatureList\u003e","```","","You can pass `icons` prop to the `FeatureList` component to display icons for each feature.","","List of available icons (extendable): `src/components/shared/feature-list/icon/icon.jsx`.","","```md","\u003cFeatureList icons={['agent', 'speedometer']}\u003e","```","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExample\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Feature List example](images/feature-list-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## Checklist","","To display a checklist, use the `CheckList` component with `CheckItem` items inside.","","```md","\u003cCheckList title=\"Checklist title\"\u003e","","\u003cCheckItem title=\"Check item 1\" href=\"#check-item-1\"\u003e","  Check item 1 description","\u003c/CheckItem\u003e","","\u003cCheckItem title=\"Check item 2\" href=\"#check-item-2\"\u003e","  Check item 2 description","\u003c/CheckItem\u003e","","\u003c/CheckList\u003e","```","","### Notes","","- Checklist options saved in the browser local storage.","- Checklists with the same `title` will use the same local storage between pages.","- If you don't pass `title`, the id will be generated from the page `slug`.","- The best practice is to use `CheckList` with the `Steps` component on the page.","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExample\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Checklist example](images/checklist-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## Images","","The images should be sourced in `public/docs` directory and be used in `.md` with the relative path, that begins with a `/` slash","","Example file structure:","","```md","├── public","│ ├── docs","│ │ ├── conceptual-guides","│ │ ├── neon_architecture_2.png // put images in a directory with the same name as the .md file","├── content","│ ├── docs","│ │ ├── conceptual-guides","│ │ ├── architecture-overview.md","```","","To display images using Markdown syntax, use the following syntax: `![alt text](image url)`. Example content in `architecture-overview.md`:","","```md","![Neon architecture diagram](/docs/conceptual-guides/neon_architecture_2.png)","```","","If you need an image without border to show an annotated piece of UI, use the `\"no-border\"` attribute as in the example below:","","```md","![Neon architecture diagram](/docs/conceptual-guides/neon_architecture_2.png 'no-border')","```","","With this approach, all images on your doc pages will be displayed both on the production and GitHub preview.","","## Definition list","","Custom `mdx` component that makes possible using [extended markdown syntax for descriptions lists](https://www.markdownguide.org/extended-syntax/#definition-lists). Fully [WCAG-compliant](https://www.w3.org/TR/WCAG20-TECHS/H40.html). It provides an accessible way to make term lists, and it's a generally good way to add structure to a text when a writer needs more than bullets and less than headings.","","The usage is pretty [straightforward](https://github.com/neondatabase/website/pull/231/commits/8f795eaf700c31794a2267fc5978c22bfc649a0c):","","```md","[comment]: \u003c\u003e (other content here)","","\u003cDefinitionList\u003e","[comment]: \u003c\u003e (required new line)","Scenario executor",": First definition",": Second definition","","Soak test",": First and only definition","","Smoke test","Another term for smoke test",": First definition for both terms",": Second definition for both terms",": ...n definition for both terms","","[Stress test](/)",": First and **only** definition for both terms with additional markup \u003cbr/\u003e Read more: [link](/)","","[comment]: \u003c\u003e (other content here)","\u003c/DefinitionList\u003e","","[comment]: \u003c\u003e (other content here)","```","","### Acceptable markup for term","","- `*italic*`","- `[link](/)`","- `**strong**` - but that doesn't make sense, by default terms appearance is already bold","- `inlineCode` - but it doesn't alter it's change in this context","","### Constraints","","- using emojis in `dt` is prohibited, as it potentially can mess up with `id` attribute, and `href` at anchor. We can not be sure which range will be used to display a particular symbol (depends on editor OS) and if it is going to be stripped.","- if there are multiple terms for a given set of descriptions, only the first one will have an `id` and an `anchor`","- make absolutely sure your `dt` text content is unique across the page to avoid `id` collisions","","### Acceptable markup for description","","- everything for term","- emojis","- any inline html","- line breaks `\u003cbr/\u003e` (recommended way to separate visually something inside a single description)","","\u003cdetails\u003e","\u003csummary\u003eExamples\u003c/summary\u003e","","![Definition list example](images/definition-list-example.jpg)","","\u003c/details\u003e","","## Detail Icon Cards","","`DetailIconCards` is a custom MDX component that displays data in a card format. Each card contains icon, title, href and description. This layout is especially useful for presenting grouped information in a visually pleasing and easy-to-understand way.","","```md","\u003cDetailIconCards\u003e","","\u003ca href=\"https://api-docs.neon.tech/reference/getting-started-with-neon-api\" description=\"Collaborate on open-source projects\" icon=\"github\"\u003eHeadless vector search\u003c/a\u003e","","\u003ca href=\"https://api-docs.neon.tech/reference/getting-started-with-neon-api\" description=\"Collaborate on open-source projects\" icon=\"github\"\u003eOpen AI completions\u003c/a\u003e","","\u003c/DetailIconCards\u003e","```","","List of available icons in folder: /website/src/components/pages/doc/detail-icon-cards/images","","## Shared MDX components","","Create a [markdown file](https://github.com/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/shared-content/need-help.md) in folder `content/docs/shared-content/`, add to `sharedMdxComponents` the name of component and the path to component.","","```js","const sharedMdxComponents = {","  // ConponentName: 'shared-content/component-filename'","  NeedHelp: 'shared-content/need-help',","};","","export default sharedMdxComponents;","```","","Insert a shared markdown and render inline.","","```md","## Resources","","- [Open AI tiktoken source code on GitHub](https://github.com/openai/tiktoken)","- [pg_tiktoken source code on GitHub](https://github.com/kelvich/pg_tiktoken)","","\u003cNeedHelp/\u003e","```","","You can pass props to the shared component:","","```md","\u003cComponentWithProps text=\"The pgvector extension\" /\u003e","```","","`component-with-props.md`","","```md","\u003cAdmonition type=\"note\" title=\"Test component with props\"\u003e","  {text}","\u003c/Admonition\u003e","```","","## CopyPrompt","","A reusable MDX component that shows a \"copy prompt\" box and lets users copy curated llm prompts from a file with one click.","","**Usage:**","","```mdx","\u003cCopyPrompt","  src=\"/prompts/serverless-driver-prompt.md\"","  displayText=\"Use this pre-built prompt to get started faster.\"","  buttonText=\"Copy prompt\"","/\u003e","```","","`src` prop is mandatory. `displayText` and `buttonText` are optional, if you want to override the defaults.","","| Prop          | Type   | Default                                            | Description                                         |","| ------------- | ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------- |","| `src`         | string | (required)                                         | Path to the markdown file or prompt content to copy |","| `displayText` | string | \"Use this pre-built prompt to get started faster.\" | CTA text shown on the left                          |","| `buttonText`  | string | \"Copy prompt\"                                      | Button label                                        |","","### Where to place prompt files","","Prompt markdown files should be placed in the `public/prompts/` directory of your project. This allows them to be fetched at runtime by the `CopyPrompt` component using a path like `/prompts/your-prompt-file.md`.","","**Example:**","","- Place your prompt file at: `public/prompts/serverless-driver-guardrail-prompt.md`","- Reference it in your MDX:","","  ```mdx","  \u003cCopyPrompt src=\"/prompts/serverless-driver-guardrail-prompt.md\" /\u003e","  ```","","## Contributing","","For small changes and spelling fixes, we recommend using the GitHub UI because Markdown files are relatively easy to edit.","","For larger contributions, consider [running the project locally](../../README.md#getting-started) to see how changes look like before making a pull request."],"stylingDirectives":[[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[[0,9,"pl-ent"],[11,37,"pl-s"],[11,12,"pl-pds"],[36,37,"pl-pds"]],[[0,3,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,6,"pl-mh"],[2,6,"pl-en"]],[],[[66,67,"pl-s"],[76,77,"pl-s"],[77,78,"pl-s"],[78,84,"pl-corl"],[84,85,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,20,"pl-mh"],[3,20,"pl-en"]],[],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,8,"pl-c1"],[8,9,"pl-s"],[109,110,"pl-s"],[110,114,"pl-c1"],[114,115,"pl-s"],[125,126,"pl-s"],[131,132,"pl-s"],[132,133,"pl-s"],[133,164,"pl-corl"],[164,165,"pl-s"],[193,194,"pl-s"],[194,207,"pl-c1"],[207,208,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[8,9,"pl-s"],[9,13,"pl-c1"],[13,14,"pl-s"],[41,42,"pl-s"],[42,43,"pl-s"],[43,57,"pl-c1"],[57,58,"pl-s"],[58,59,"pl-s"],[59,60,"pl-s"],[60,87,"pl-corl"],[87,88,"pl-s"],[98,99,"pl-s"],[99,103,"pl-c1"],[103,104,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[27,28,"pl-s"],[28,30,"pl-c1"],[30,31,"pl-s"],[105,106,"pl-s"],[106,111,"pl-c1"],[111,112,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,9,"pl-mh"],[3,9,"pl-en"]],[],[],[],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,9,"pl-c1"],[9,10,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,12,"pl-c1"],[12,13,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,7,"pl-c1"],[7,8,"pl-s"],[61,62,"pl-s"],[62,65,"pl-c1"],[65,66,"pl-s"],[68,69,"pl-s"],[69,73,"pl-c1"],[73,74,"pl-s"],[76,77,"pl-s"],[77,88,"pl-c1"],[88,89,"pl-s"],[91,92,"pl-s"],[92,102,"pl-c1"],[102,103,"pl-s"],[164,165,"pl-s"],[165,180,"pl-c1"],[180,181,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,16,"pl-c1"],[16,17,"pl-s"],[125,126,"pl-s"],[126,141,"pl-c1"],[141,142,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,11,"pl-c1"],[11,12,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,25,"pl-c1"],[25,26,"pl-s"],[152,153,"pl-s"],[153,154,"pl-s"],[154,156,"pl-c1"],[156,157,"pl-s"],[159,160,"pl-s"],[160,162,"pl-c1"],[162,163,"pl-s"],[163,164,"pl-s"]],[[0,1,"pl-s"],[1,2,"pl-v"],[3,4,"pl-s"],[4,11,"pl-c1"],[11,12,"pl-s"]],[],[[0,112,"pl-ent"],[0,2,"pl-ent"]],[[0,0,"pl-ent"]],[[0,13,"pl-mh"] <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Docs</h1><a id="user-content-docs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Docs" href="#docs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Welcome to Neon docs! This folder contains the source code of the <a href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/docs">Neon docs</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Basic information</h2><a id="user-content-basic-information" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Basic information" href="#basic-information"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Every single Markdown file in this folder will be turned into a docs page.</li>
<li>Folder and file names should follow kebab-case.</li>
<li><code>slug</code> is generated based on the folder structure and file names inside this folder. In order to see page <code>slug</code>, you can <a href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/README.md#run-the-website">start</a> and build the project with <code>npm run build</code> command that will display all generated pages.</li>
<li>Page <code>path</code> is generated by combining <a href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/src/constants/docs.js"><code>DOCS_BASE_PATH</code></a> and page <code>slug</code>.</li>
<li>There is no need to add <code>h1</code> to the page since it will be displayed automatically with the value from <code>title</code> field.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fields</h2><a id="user-content-fields" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fields" href="#fields"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Right now Markdown files accept the following fields:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><code>title</code> — title of the page (required)</li>
<li><code>subTitle</code> — subtitle of the page.</li>
<li><code>tag</code> — tag for the page. It can be one of the following: <code>new</code>, <code>beta</code>, <code>coming soon</code>, <code>deprecated</code>, or you can use your own tag. Don't forget to add it to the <code>navigation.yaml</code> file as well.</li>
<li><code>redirectFrom</code> — array of strings with paths to redirect from to the page, should start and end with a slash, for example <code>/docs/old-path/</code></li>
<li><code>isDraft</code> — flag that says the page is not ready yet. It won't appear in production but will appear in the development mode.</li>
<li><code>enableTableOfContents</code> — flag that turns on the display of the outline for the page. The outline gets built out of second and third-level headings ([<code>h2</code>, <code>h3</code>]), thus appears as two-level nested max.</li>
<li><code>ogImage</code> - the social preview image of the page.</li>
</ol>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> Please note that the project won't build if at least one of the Markdown files is missing a required field.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Navigation</h2><a id="user-content-navigation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Navigation" href="#navigation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Navigation data is stored in the <a href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/navigation.yaml">navigation.yaml</a> file.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Navigation Structure</h3><a id="user-content-navigation-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Navigation Structure" href="#navigation-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The navigation system is a unified structure where:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Top-level items</strong> appear in the header navigation</li>
<li><strong>Child items</strong> appear in the left sidebar</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">This creates a seamless navigation experience where users select a main category from the header and see its detailed structure in the sidebar.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Top Navigation Structure</h3><a id="user-content-top-navigation-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Top Navigation Structure" href="#top-navigation-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Each top-level navigation item has the following structure:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="- nav: Get started # Navigation label (displayed in header)
  slug: introduction # URL slug for the section
  title: Neon Docs # Page title
  icon: home # Icon identifier
  subnav: # Sub-navigation items for header dropdowns
    - title: Neon platform
      slug: manage/platform
      icon: settings
      items: # Sidebar navigation items
        ..."><pre>- <span class="pl-ent">nav</span>: <span class="pl-s">Get started </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Navigation label (displayed in header)</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">introduction </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> URL slug for the section</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Neon Docs </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Page title</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">icon</span>: <span class="pl-s">home </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Icon identifier</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">subnav</span>: <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Sub-navigation items for header dropdowns</span>
    - <span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Neon platform</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">manage/platform</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">icon</span>: <span class="pl-s">settings</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">items</span>: <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Sidebar navigation items</span>
        <span class="pl-s">...</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Important</strong>: Top-level items can contain either:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>subnav</code></strong>: Sub-navigation items that appear as header dropdowns</li>
<li><strong><code>items</code></strong>: Navigation items that appear in the sidebar</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sidebar Navigation Structure</h3><a id="user-content-sidebar-navigation-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sidebar Navigation Structure" href="#sidebar-navigation-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The sidebar navigation supports multiple levels:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  ...
  items: # Sidebar navigation items
    - section: Features # Section header
      icon: features
      slug: guides/neon-features
      items: # Section items
        - title: Serverless
          slug: introduction/serverless
        - title: Autoscaling
          slug: introduction/autoscaling
          items: # Section subitems
            - title: Introduction
              slug: introduction/autoscaling
            - title: Architecture
              slug: introduction/autoscaling-architecture"><pre>  <span class="pl-s">...</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">items</span>: <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Sidebar navigation items</span>
    - <span class="pl-ent">section</span>: <span class="pl-s">Features </span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Section header</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">icon</span>: <span class="pl-s">features</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">guides/neon-features</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">items</span>: <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Section items</span>
        - <span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Serverless</span>
          <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">introduction/serverless</span>
        - <span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Autoscaling</span>
          <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">introduction/autoscaling</span>
          <span class="pl-ent">items</span>: <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Section subitems</span>
            - <span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Introduction</span>
              <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">introduction/autoscaling</span>
            - <span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Architecture</span>
              <span class="pl-ent">slug</span>: <span class="pl-s">introduction/autoscaling-architecture</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to add a new top navigation category</h3><a id="user-content-how-to-add-a-new-top-navigation-category" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to add a new top navigation category" href="#how-to-add-a-new-top-navigation-category"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add a new top-level navigation category, add a new item to the top level array with keys <code>nav</code>, <code>slug</code>, <code>title</code>, <code>icon</code>, and optionally <code>items</code> or <code>subnav</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-diff notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="+- nav: New Category
+  slug: new-category
+  title: New Category Title
+  icon: new-icon
+  subnav:
+    ..."><pre><span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>- nav: New Category</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>  slug: new-category</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>  title: New Category Title</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>  icon: new-icon</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>  subnav:</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>    ...</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to add a new section</h3><a id="user-content-how-to-add-a-new-section" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to add a new section" href="#how-to-add-a-new-section"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add a new section within a navigation category, add a new item with keys <code>section</code>, <code>icon</code>, and <code>items</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-diff notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  ...
  items:
+   - section: Architecture
+     icon: architecture
+     items:
+       ..."><pre>  ...
  items:
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>   - section: Architecture</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>     icon: architecture</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>     items:</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>       ...</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How to add a new page</h3><a id="user-content-how-to-add-a-new-page" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to add a new page" href="#how-to-add-a-new-page"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To add a new page, add a new item with keys <code>title</code> and <code>slug</code> under the appropriate section or navigation level.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-diff notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  ...
  items:
+   - title: Overview
+     slug: introduction/architecture-overview"><pre>  ...
  items:
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>   - title: Overview</span>
<span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span>     slug: introduction/architecture-overview</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Navigation Properties</h3><a id="user-content-navigation-properties" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Navigation Properties" href="#navigation-properties"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>nav</code>: The label displayed in the top navigation header</li>
<li><code>slug</code>: The URL path for the page/section</li>
<li><code>title</code>: The display title for the page/section</li>
<li><code>icon</code>: Icon identifier for visual representation</li>
<li><code>section</code>: Section header for grouping related items</li>
<li><code>items</code>: Array of navigation items</li>
<li><code>subnav</code>: Sub-navigation items for the sidebar</li>
<li><code>tag</code>: Optional tag (for example, "new", "beta") displayed next to the title</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Important Notes</h3><a id="user-content-important-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Important Notes" href="#important-notes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>title</code> in the sidebar may differ from <code>title</code> in the Markdown file</li>
<li><code>slug</code> should always match the page's slug</li>
<li>The navigation supports unlimited nesting levels for complex documentation structures</li>
<li>Icons are referenced by name and should match available icon components</li>
<li>Tags like "new" or "beta" are automatically displayed with special styling</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Code blocks</h2><a id="user-content-code-blocks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Code blocks" href="#code-blocks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All available languages for code blocks can be found <a href="https://shiki.matsu.io/languages" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can use fenced code blocks with three backticks (```) on the lines before and after the code block. And display code with options</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">enable highlighting single lines, multiple lines, and ranges of code lines</p>
<p dir="auto">Examples:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Single line highlight</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```c++ {1}
#include &lt;iostream&gt;

int main() {
    std::cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Hello World&quot;;
    return 0;
}
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">c++</span> {1}
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-c1">std::cout &lt;&lt; "Hello World";</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">return 0;</span>
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Multiple lines</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```c++ {1,2,5}
#include &lt;iostream&gt;

int main() {
    std::cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Hello World&quot;;
    return 0;
}
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">c++</span> {1,2,5}
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-c1">std::cout &lt;&lt; "Hello World";</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">return 0;</span>
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Range of code lines</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```c++ {1-3,5}
#include &lt;iostream&gt;

int main() {
    std::cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Hello World&quot;;
    return 0;
}
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">c++</span> {1-3,5}
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-c1">std::cout &lt;&lt; "Hello World";</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">return 0;</span>
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">use <code>[!code highlight]</code> to highlight a line.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export function foo() {
  console.log('Highlighted'); // [!code highlight]
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Highlighted'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// [!code highlight]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">use <code>[!code word:xxx]</code> to highlight a word.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export function foo() {
  // [!code word:Hello]
  const msg = 'Hello World';
  console.log(msg);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// [!code word:Hello]</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">msg</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Hello World'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">msg</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">use <code>[!code --]</code> and <code>[!code ++]</code> to highlight a code diff.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-ts notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export function foo() {
  const msg = 'Hello Word'; // [!code --]
  const msg = 'Hello World'; // [!code ++]
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">foo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">msg</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Hello Word'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// [!code --]</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">msg</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'Hello World'</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// [!code ++]</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>showLineNumbers</code> - flag to show on the line numbers in the code block.</p>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```c++ showLineNumbers
#include &lt;iostream&gt;

int main() {
    std::cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Hello World&quot;;
    return 0;
}
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">c++</span> showLineNumbers
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-c1">std::cout &lt;&lt; "Hello World";</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">return 0;</span>
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>shouldWrap</code> - flag to enable code wrapping in the code block.</p>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```powershell shouldWrap
powershell -Command &quot;Start-Process -FilePath powershell -Verb RunAs -ArgumentList '-NoProfile','-InputFormat None','-ExecutionPolicy Bypass','-Command &quot;&quot;iex (iwr -UseBasicParsing https://cli.configu.com/install.ps1)&quot;&quot;'&quot;
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">powershell</span> shouldWrap<span class="pl-c1"></span>
<span class="pl-c1">powershell -Command "Start-Process -FilePath powershell -Verb RunAs -ArgumentList '-NoProfile','-InputFormat None','-ExecutionPolicy Bypass','-Command ""iex (iwr -UseBasicParsing https://cli.configu.com/install.ps1)""'"</span>
<span class="pl-c1"></span><span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>filename="..."</code> - add a filename label above the code block.</p>
<p dir="auto">Examples:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```jsx filename=&quot;src/App.jsx&quot;
export default function App() {
  return &lt;div&gt;Hello&lt;/div&gt;;
}
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">jsx</span> filename="src/App.jsx"
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-c1">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">App</span>() {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>div<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>Hello<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">/</span>div<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>;
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can combine it with line highlighting and other flags:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="```jsx filename=&quot;src/App.jsx&quot; {2} showLineNumbers shouldWrap
export default function App() {
  return &lt;div&gt;Hello&lt;/div&gt;;
}
```"><pre><span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">jsx</span> filename="src/App.jsx" {2} showLineNumbers shouldWrap
<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-c1">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">App</span>() {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>div<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>Hello<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">/</span>div<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>;
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Code Tabs</h2><a id="user-content-code-tabs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Code Tabs" href="#code-tabs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To display code tabs, wrap all pieces of code with <code>&lt;CodeTabs&gt;&lt;/CodeTabs&gt;</code> and write labels of code tabs in order:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;CodeTabs labels={[&quot;Shell&quot;, &quot;C++&quot;, &quot;C#&quot;, &quot;Java&quot;]}&gt;

```bash {2-4}
#!/bin/bash
STR=&quot;Hello World!&quot;
echo $STR
```

```c++
#include &lt;iostream&gt;

int main() {
    std::cout &lt;&lt; &quot;Hello World&quot;;
    return 0;
}
```

```csharp
namespace HelloWorld
{
    class Hello {
        static void Main(string[] args)
        {
            System.Console.WriteLine(&quot;Hello World&quot;);
        }
    }
}
```

```java
import java.io.*;

class GFG {
    public static void main (String[] args) {
       System.out.println(&quot;Hello World&quot;);
    }
}
```

&lt;/CodeTabs&gt;"><pre>&lt;CodeTabs labels={<span class="pl-s">[</span>"Shell", "C++", "C#", "Java"<span class="pl-s">]</span>}&gt;

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">bash</span> {2-4}
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#!</span>/bin/bash</span>
STR=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hello World!<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-smi">$STR</span>
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">c++</span>
#<span class="pl-k">include</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;</span>iostream<span class="pl-pds">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="pl-k">int</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-c1">std::cout &lt;&lt; "Hello World";</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">return 0;</span>
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">csharp</span>
<span class="pl-k">namespace</span> <span class="pl-en">HelloWorld</span>
{
    <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">Hello</span> {
        <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">Main</span>(<span class="pl-k">string</span>[] <span class="pl-en">args</span>)
        {
            <span class="pl-smi">System</span>.<span class="pl-smi">Console</span>.<span class="pl-en">WriteLine</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hello World<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
        }
    }
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">java</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-smi">java.io.*</span>;

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">GFG</span> {
    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span> (<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
       <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Hello World<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
    }
}
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">CodeTabs</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<details>
<summary>Examples</summary>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/code-tabs-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/code-tabs-example.jpg" alt="Code tabs example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">External Code</h2><a id="user-content-external-code" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: External Code" href="#external-code"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>ExternalCode</code> component allows embedding code content from external sources with syntax highlighting.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage</h3><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;ExternalCode
  url=&quot;https://raw.githubusercontent.com/neondatabase/neon/main/README.md&quot;
/&gt;"><pre>&lt;ExternalCode
  url="<span class="pl-corl">https://raw.githubusercontent.com/neondatabase/neon/main/README.md</span>"

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Props</h3><a id="user-content-props" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Props" href="#props"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Prop</th>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Default</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>url</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>(required)</td>
<td>URL to the raw file</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>language</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>(optional)</td>
<td>Language for syntax highlighting (defaults to file extension)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>shouldWrap</td>
<td>boolean</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>Enables code wrapping in the code block</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>showLineNumbers</td>
<td>boolean</td>
<td>false</td>
<td>Shows line numbers in the code block</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>className</td>
<td>string</td>
<td>''</td>
<td>Additional CSS classes to apply to the component</td>
</tr>
