<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Best Practices</h3><a id="user-content-best-practices" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Best Practices" href="#best-practices"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Always use raw URLs from the GitHub repository (for example, <code>https://raw.githubusercontent.com/...</code>).</li>
<li>Use the <code>language</code> prop when the file extension doesn't match the actual content type.</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Tabs</h2><a id="user-content-tabs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Tabs" href="#tabs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To display the tabs with content as image, video, code block, .etc, wrap the <code>TabItem</code> with <code>Tabs</code></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;Tabs labels={[&quot;Content&quot;, &quot;CLI&quot;]}&gt;

&lt;TabItem&gt;
In your config v3 project, head to the `/metadata/databases/databases.yaml` file and add the database configuration as below.

```bash showLineNumbers
- name: &lt;db_name&gt;
  kind: postgres
  configuration:
    connection_info:
      database_url:
        from_env: &lt;DB_URL_ENV_VAR&gt;
    pool_settings:
      idle_timeout: 180
      max_connections: 50
      retries: 1
  tables: []
  functions: []
```

Apply the Metadata by running:

```bash
hasura metadata apply
```

If you've spun up the Hasura Engine with Docker, you can access the Hasura Console by accessing it in a browser at the URL of your Hasura Engine instance, usually http://localhost:8080.

&lt;Admonition type=&quot;note&quot;&gt;
To access the Hasura Console via the URL the HASURA_GRAPHQL_ENABLE_CONSOLE environment variable or the `--enable-console` flag must be set to true.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;

&lt;/TabItem&gt;

&lt;TabItem&gt;
Alternatively, you can create read replicas using the Neon API or Neon CLI.

```bash
curl --request POST \
     --url https://console.neon.tech/api/v2/projects/late-bar-27572981/endpoints \
     --header 'Accept: application/json' \
     --header &quot;Authorization: Bearer $NEON_API_KEY&quot; \
     --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
     --data '
{
  &quot;endpoint&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;read_only&quot;,
    &quot;branch_id&quot;: &quot;br-young-fire-15282225&quot;
  }
}
' | jq
```

&lt;/TabItem&gt;

&lt;/Tabs&gt;"><pre>&lt;Tabs labels={<span class="pl-s">[</span>"Content", "CLI"<span class="pl-s">]</span>}&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">TabItem</span>&gt;
In your config v3 project, head to the <span class="pl-s">`</span><span class="pl-c1">/metadata/databases/databases.yaml</span><span class="pl-s">`</span> file and add the database configuration as below.

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">bash</span> showLineNumbers
- name: <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>db_name<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
  kind: postgres
  configuration:
    connection_info:
      database_url:
        from_env: <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>DB_URL_ENV_VAR<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
    pool_settings:
      idle_timeout: 180
      max_connections: 50
      retries: 1
  tables: []
  functions: []
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

Apply the Metadata by running:

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">bash</span>
hasura metadata apply
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

If you've spun up the Hasura Engine with Docker, you can access the Hasura Console by accessing it in a browser at the URL of your Hasura Engine instance, usually <span class="pl-corl">http://localhost:8080</span>.

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">note</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
To access the Hasura Console via the URL the HASURA_GRAPHQL_ENABLE_CONSOLE environment variable or the <span class="pl-s">`</span><span class="pl-c1">--enable-console</span><span class="pl-s">`</span> flag must be set to true.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">TabItem</span>&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">TabItem</span>&gt;
Alternatively, you can create read replicas using the Neon API or Neon CLI.

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">bash</span>
curl --request POST \
     --url https://console.neon.tech/api/v2/projects/late-bar-27572981/endpoints \
     --header <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Accept: application/json<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
     --header <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Authorization: Bearer <span class="pl-smi">$NEON_API_KEY</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
     --header <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Content-Type: application/json<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
     --data <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">{</span>
<span class="pl-s">  "endpoint": {</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "type": "read_only",</span>
<span class="pl-s">    "branch_id": "br-young-fire-15282225"</span>
<span class="pl-s">  }</span>
<span class="pl-s">}</span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> jq
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">TabItem</span>&gt;

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Tabs</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Admonition</h2><a id="user-content-admonition" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Admonition" href="#admonition"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To improve the documentation readability, one can leverage an Admonition custom component. Just wrap your piece of text with <code>&lt;Admonition&gt;&lt;/Admonition&gt;</code> and pass the type.</p>
<p dir="auto">There are 6 types of Admonition: <code>note</code>, <code>important</code>, <code>tip</code>, <code>info</code>, <code>warning</code>, <code>comingSoon</code>; the default is <code>note</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">You may also specify an optional title with prop <code>title</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;Admonition type=&quot;note&quot;&gt;
Highlights information that users should take into account, even when skimming.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;

&lt;Admonition type=&quot;important&quot;&gt;
Crucial information necessary for users to succeed.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;

&lt;Admonition type=&quot;tip&quot;&gt;
Optional information to help a user be more successful.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;

&lt;Admonition type=&quot;info&quot;&gt;
Information that helps users understand the things better.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;

&lt;Admonition type=&quot;warning&quot;&gt;
Critical content demanding immediate user attention due to potential risks.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;

&lt;Admonition type=&quot;comingSoon&quot;&gt;
Information about features that are coming soon.
&lt;/Admonition&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">note</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Highlights information that users should take into account, even when skimming.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">important</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Crucial information necessary for users to succeed.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">tip</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Optional information to help a user be more successful.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">info</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Information that helps users understand the things better.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">warning</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Critical content demanding immediate user attention due to potential risks.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">comingSoon</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Information about features that are coming soon.
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<details>
<summary>Examples</summary>

</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CTA</h2><a id="user-content-cta" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CTA" href="#cta"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This is a simple block with title, description text and one CTA button that accomplish certain actions.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;CTA /&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">CTA</span> /&gt;</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Check the example for default data of CTA block</p>
<details>
<summary>Example</summary>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/cta-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/cta-example.jpg" alt="CTA example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</details>
<p dir="auto">To change text in CTA block, you can pass to the component props <code>title</code>, <code>description</code>, <code>buttonText</code>, <code>buttonUrl</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;CTA title=&quot;Try it on Neon!&quot; description=&quot;Neon is Serverless Postgres built for the cloud. Explore Postgres features and functions in our user-friendly SQL Editor. Sign up for a free account to get started.&quot; buttonText=&quot;Sign Up&quot; buttonUrl=&quot;https://console.neon.tech/signup&quot; /&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">CTA</span> <span class="pl-e">title</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">Try it on Neon!</span><span class="pl-s">"</span> <span class="pl-e">description</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">Neon is Serverless Postgres built for the cloud. Explore Postgres features and functions in our user-friendly SQL Editor. Sign up for a free account to get started.</span><span class="pl-s">"</span> <span class="pl-e">buttonText</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">Sign Up</span><span class="pl-s">"</span> <span class="pl-e">buttonUrl</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">https://console.neon.tech/signup</span><span class="pl-s">"</span> /&gt;</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Steps</h2><a id="user-content-steps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Steps" href="#steps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To display numbered steps, wrap the content with <code>Steps</code> component.<br>
Steps will be splitted by <code>h2</code> headings.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;Steps&gt;

## Step 1: Create the Initial Schema

First, create a new database called `people` on the `main` branch and add some sample data to it.

## Step 2: Create a development branch

Create a new development branch off of `main`. This branch will be an exact, isolated copy of `main`.

&lt;/Steps&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Steps</span>&gt;

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Step 1: Create the Initial Schema</span></span>

First, create a new database called <span class="pl-s">`</span><span class="pl-c1">people</span><span class="pl-s">`</span> on the <span class="pl-s">`</span><span class="pl-c1">main</span><span class="pl-s">`</span> branch and add some sample data to it.

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Step 2: Create a development branch</span></span>

Create a new development branch off of <span class="pl-s">`</span><span class="pl-c1">main</span><span class="pl-s">`</span>. This branch will be an exact, isolated copy of <span class="pl-s">`</span><span class="pl-c1">main</span><span class="pl-s">`</span>.

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Steps</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<details>
<summary>Example</summary>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/steps-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/steps-example.jpg" alt="Steps example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Two Column Layout</h2><a id="user-content-two-column-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Two Column Layout" href="#two-column-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>TwoColumnLayout</code> component creates a two-column layout for tutorial pages and reference documentation. Use <code>TwoColumnLayout.Step</code> for numbered tutorial steps or <code>TwoColumnLayout.Item</code> for default items. Nested content blocks should be wrapped with <code>TwoColumnLayout.Block</code>.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note:</strong> Pages using <code>TwoColumnLayout</code> should include <code>layout: wide</code> prop to hide the right sidebar (Table of Contents) and provide more space for the two-column layout.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Check <a href="https://neon.com/docs/auth/quick-start/nextjs-api-only" rel="nofollow">Neon Auth with Next.js</a> and <a href="https://neon.com/docs/reference/javascript-sdk" rel="nofollow">Neon TypeScript SDK</a> for usage examples.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;TwoColumnLayout&gt;

&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Step title=&quot;Install dependencies&quot;&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;

Install the required packages for your project.

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block label=&quot;Terminal&quot;&gt;

```bash
npm install @neondatabase/neon-js
```

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Step&gt;

&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Item title=&quot;Sign in with email&quot; method=&quot;auth.signIn.email()&quot; id=&quot;signin-email&quot;&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;

Authenticate a user with their email and password.

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;

```typescript
await client.auth.signIn.email({
  email: 'user@example.com',
  password: 'password123',
});
```

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Item&gt;

&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Footer&gt;
&lt;Admonition type=&quot;note&quot;&gt;
Additional information that spans both columns
&lt;/Admonition&gt;
&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Footer&gt;

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">TwoColumnLayout</span>&gt;

&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Step title="Install dependencies"&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;

Install the required packages for your project.

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block label="Terminal"&gt;

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">bash</span>
npm install @neondatabase/neon-js
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Step&gt;

&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Item title="Sign in with email" method="auth.signIn.email()" id="signin-email"&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;

Authenticate a user with their email and password.

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;

<span class="pl-s">```</span><span class="pl-en">typescript</span>
<span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-smi">client</span>.<span class="pl-smi">auth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">signIn</span>.<span class="pl-en">email</span>({
  email: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>user@example.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  password: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>password123<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
});
<span class="pl-s">```</span>

&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Block&gt;
&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Item&gt;

&lt;TwoColumnLayout.Footer&gt;
&lt;<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span> <span class="pl-e">type</span>=<span class="pl-s">"</span><span class="pl-s">note</span><span class="pl-s">"</span>&gt;
Additional information that spans both columns
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">Admonition</span>&gt;
&lt;/TwoColumnLayout.Footer&gt;

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">TwoColumnLayout</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Components:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>TwoColumnLayout.Step</code> - Numbered step with <code>title</code> prop (for tutorials)</li>
<li><code>TwoColumnLayout.Item</code> - Default item with <code>title</code>, <code>method</code>, and <code>id</code> prop</li>
<li><code>TwoColumnLayout.Block</code> - Nested content block with optional <code>label</code> prop</li>
<li><code>TwoColumnLayout.Footer</code> - Full-width content at the bottom of a step</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary>Examples</summary>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/two-column-layout-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/two-column-layout-example.jpg" alt="Two Column Layout example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Example with steps:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/two-column-layout-steps-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/two-column-layout-steps-example.jpg" alt="Two Column Layout example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Feature List</h2><a id="user-content-feature-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Feature List" href="#feature-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To display a list of features, use the <code>FeatureList</code> component.
Features will be splitted by <code>h2</code> and <code>h3</code> headings.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;FeatureList&gt;

### Agent creates an app

A vibe coder imagines an app. Your agent builds it, full-stack.

### Gets a working database instantly, with no friction

Neon provisions the database behind the scenes via API.

&lt;/FeatureList&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">FeatureList</span>&gt;

<span class="pl-mh">### <span class="pl-en">Agent creates an app</span></span>

A vibe coder imagines an app. Your agent builds it, full-stack.

<span class="pl-mh">### <span class="pl-en">Gets a working database instantly, with no friction</span></span>

Neon provisions the database behind the scenes via API.

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">FeatureList</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can pass <code>icons</code> prop to the <code>FeatureList</code> component to display icons for each feature.</p>
<p dir="auto">List of available icons (extendable): <code>src/components/shared/feature-list/icon/icon.jsx</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;FeatureList icons={['agent', 'speedometer']}&gt;"><pre>&lt;FeatureList icons={<span class="pl-s">[</span>'agent', 'speedometer'<span class="pl-s">]</span>}&gt;</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Checklist</h2><a id="user-content-checklist" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Checklist" href="#checklist"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To display a checklist, use the <code>CheckList</code> component with <code>CheckItem</code> items inside.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;CheckList title=&quot;Checklist title&quot;&gt;

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Notes</h3><a id="user-content-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Notes" href="#notes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Checklist options saved in the browser local storage.</li>
<li>Checklists with the same <code>title</code> will use the same local storage between pages.</li>
<li>If you don't pass <code>title</code>, the id will be generated from the page <code>slug</code>.</li>
<li>The best practice is to use <code>CheckList</code> with the <code>Steps</code> component on the page.</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary>Example</summary>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/checklist-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/checklist-example.jpg" alt="Checklist example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Images</h2><a id="user-content-images" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Images" href="#images"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The images should be sourced in <code>public/docs</code> directory and be used in <code>.md</code> with the relative path, that begins with a <code>/</code> slash</p>
<p dir="auto">Example file structure:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="├── public
│ ├── docs
│ │ ├── conceptual-guides
│ │ ├── neon_architecture_2.png // put images in a directory with the same name as the .md file
├── content
│ ├── docs
│ │ ├── conceptual-guides
│ │ ├── architecture-overview.md"><pre>├── public
│ ├── docs
│ │ ├── conceptual-guides
│ │ ├── neon_architecture_2.png // put images in a directory with the same name as the .md file
├── content
│ ├── docs
│ │ ├── conceptual-guides
│ │ ├── architecture-overview.md</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">To display images using Markdown syntax, use the following syntax: <code>![alt text](image url)</code>. Example content in <code>architecture-overview.md</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="![Neon architecture diagram](/docs/conceptual-guides/neon_architecture_2.png)"><pre><span class="pl-s">![</span>Neon architecture diagram<span class="pl-s">]</span><span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-corl">/docs/conceptual-guides/neon_architecture_2.png</span><span class="pl-s">)</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If you need an image without border to show an annotated piece of UI, use the <code>"no-border"</code> attribute as in the example below:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="![Neon architecture diagram](/docs/conceptual-guides/neon_architecture_2.png 'no-border')"><pre><span class="pl-s">![</span>Neon architecture diagram<span class="pl-s">]</span><span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-corl">/docs/conceptual-guides/neon_architecture_2.png</span> <span class="pl-s">'</span><span class="pl-s">no-border</span><span class="pl-s">')</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">With this approach, all images on your doc pages will be displayed both on the production and GitHub preview.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Definition list</h2><a id="user-content-definition-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Definition list" href="#definition-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Custom <code>mdx</code> component that makes possible using <a href="https://www.markdownguide.org/extended-syntax/#definition-lists" rel="nofollow">extended markdown syntax for descriptions lists</a>. Fully <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/WCAG20-TECHS/H40.html" rel="nofollow">WCAG-compliant</a>. It provides an accessible way to make term lists, and it's a generally good way to add structure to a text when a writer needs more than bullets and less than headings.</p>
<p dir="auto">The usage is pretty <a href="https://github.com/neondatabase/website/pull/231/commits/8f795eaf700c31794a2267fc5978c22bfc649a0c">straightforward</a>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[comment]: &lt;&gt; (other content here)

&lt;DefinitionList&gt;
[comment]: &lt;&gt; (required new line)
Scenario executor
: First definition
: Second definition

Soak test
: First and only definition

Smoke test
Another term for smoke test
: First definition for both terms
: Second definition for both terms
: ...n definition for both terms

[Stress test](/)
: First and **only** definition for both terms with additional markup &lt;br/&gt; Read more: [link](/)

[comment]: &lt;&gt; (other content here)
&lt;/DefinitionList&gt;

[comment]: &lt;&gt; (other content here)"><pre><span class="pl-s">[</span><span class="pl-en">comment</span><span class="pl-s">]</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-s">other content here</span><span class="pl-s">)</span>

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">DefinitionList</span>&gt;
<span class="pl-s">[</span><span class="pl-en">comment</span><span class="pl-s">]</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-s">required new line</span><span class="pl-s">)</span>
Scenario executor
: First definition
: Second definition

Soak test
: First and only definition

Smoke test
Another term for smoke test
: First definition for both terms
: Second definition for both terms
: ...n definition for both terms

<span class="pl-s">[</span>Stress test<span class="pl-s">]</span><span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-corl">/</span><span class="pl-s">)</span>
: First and <span class="pl-s">**</span>only<span class="pl-s">**</span> definition for both terms with additional markup &lt;<span class="pl-ent">br</span>/&gt; Read more: <span class="pl-s">[</span>link<span class="pl-s">]</span><span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-corl">/</span><span class="pl-s">)</span>

<span class="pl-s">[</span><span class="pl-en">comment</span><span class="pl-s">]</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-s">other content here</span><span class="pl-s">)</span>
&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">DefinitionList</span>&gt;

<span class="pl-s">[</span><span class="pl-en">comment</span><span class="pl-s">]</span>: <span class="pl-s">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s">(</span><span class="pl-s">other content here</span><span class="pl-s">)</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Acceptable markup for term</h3><a id="user-content-acceptable-markup-for-term" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Acceptable markup for term" href="#acceptable-markup-for-term"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>*italic*</code></li>
<li><code>[link](/)</code></li>
<li><code>**strong**</code> - but that doesn't make sense, by default terms appearance is already bold</li>
<li><code>inlineCode</code> - but it doesn't alter it's change in this context</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Constraints</h3><a id="user-content-constraints" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Constraints" href="#constraints"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>using emojis in <code>dt</code> is prohibited, as it potentially can mess up with <code>id</code> attribute, and <code>href</code> at anchor. We can not be sure which range will be used to display a particular symbol (depends on editor OS) and if it is going to be stripped.</li>
<li>if there are multiple terms for a given set of descriptions, only the first one will have an <code>id</code> and an <code>anchor</code></li>
<li>make absolutely sure your <code>dt</code> text content is unique across the page to avoid <code>id</code> collisions</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Acceptable markup for description</h3><a id="user-content-acceptable-markup-for-description" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Acceptable markup for description" href="#acceptable-markup-for-description"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>everything for term</li>
<li>emojis</li>
<li>any inline html</li>
<li>line breaks <code>&lt;br/&gt;</code> (recommended way to separate visually something inside a single description)</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary>Examples</summary>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/images/definition-list-example.jpg"><img src="/neondatabase/website/raw/main/content/docs/images/definition-list-example.jpg" alt="Definition list example" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Detail Icon Cards</h2><a id="user-content-detail-icon-cards" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Detail Icon Cards" href="#detail-icon-cards"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>DetailIconCards</code> is a custom MDX component that displays data in a card format. Each card contains icon, title, href and description. This layout is especially useful for presenting grouped information in a visually pleasing and easy-to-understand way.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;DetailIconCards&gt;

&lt;a href=&quot;https://api-docs.neon.tech/reference/getting-started-with-neon-api&quot; description=&quot;Collaborate on open-source projects&quot; icon=&quot;github&quot;&gt;Headless vector search&lt;/a&gt;

&lt;a href=&quot;https://api-docs.neon.tech/reference/getting-started-with-neon-api&quot; description=&quot;Collaborate on open-source projects&quot; icon=&quot;github&quot;&gt;Open AI completions&lt;/a&gt;

&lt;/DetailIconCards&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-ent">DetailIconCards</span>&gt;

&lt;/<span class="pl-ent">DetailIconCards</span>&gt;</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">List of available icons in folder: /website/src/components/pages/doc/detail-icon-cards/images</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Shared MDX components</h2><a id="user-content-shared-mdx-components" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Shared MDX components" href="#shared-mdx-components"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a <a href="https://github.com/neondatabase/website/blob/main/content/docs/shared-content/need-help.md">markdown file</a> in folder <code>content/docs/shared-content/</code>, add to <code>sharedMdxComponents</code> the name of component and the path to component.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const sharedMdxComponents = {
  // ConponentName: 'shared-content/component-filename'
  NeedHelp: 'shared-content/need-help',
};

export default sharedMdxComponents;"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">sharedMdxComponents</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ConponentName: 'shared-content/component-filename'</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">NeedHelp</span>: <span class="pl-s">'shared-content/need-help'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-s1">sharedMdxComponents</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Insert a shared markdown and render inline.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="## Resources

&lt;<span class="pl-ent">NeedHelp</span>/&gt;</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">CopyPrompt</h2><a id="user-content-copyprompt" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: CopyPrompt" href="#copyprompt"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A reusable MDX component that shows a "copy prompt" box and lets users copy curated llm prompts from a file with one click.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-mdx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;CopyPrompt
  src=&quot;/prompts/serverless-driver-prompt.md&quot;
  displayText=&quot;Use this pre-built prompt to get started faster.&quot;
  buttonText=&quot;Copy prompt&quot;
/&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">CopyPrompt</span>
  <span class="pl-e">src</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/prompts/serverless-driver-prompt.md<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-e">displayText</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Use this pre-built prompt to get started faster.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-e">buttonText</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Copy prompt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
/&gt;</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>src</code> prop is mandatory. <code>displayText</code> and <code>buttonText</code> are optional, if you want to override the defaults.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Prop</th>
<th>Type</th>
<th>Default</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>src</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>(required)</td>
<td>Path to the markdown file or prompt content to copy</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>displayText</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>"Use this pre-built prompt to get started faster."</td>
<td>CTA text shown on the left</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>buttonText</code></td>
<td>string</td>
<td>"Copy prompt"</td>
<td>Button label</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Where to place prompt files</h3><a id="user-content-where-to-place-prompt-files" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Where to place prompt files" href="#where-to-place-prompt-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Prompt markdown files should be placed in the <code>public/prompts/</code> directory of your project. This allows them to be fetched at runtime by the <code>CopyPrompt</code> component using a path like <code>/prompts/your-prompt-file.md</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Place your prompt file at: <code>public/prompts/serverless-driver-guardrail-prompt.md</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Reference it in your MDX:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-mdx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;CopyPrompt src=&quot;/prompts/serverless-driver-guardrail-prompt.md&quot; /&gt;"><pre>&lt;<span class="pl-c1">CopyPrompt</span> <span class="pl-e">src</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/prompts/serverless-driver-guardrail-prompt.md<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> /&gt;</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Contributing</h2><a id="user-content-contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Contributing" href="#contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For small changes and spelling fixes, we recommend using the GitHub UI because Markdown files are relatively easy to edit.</p>
<p dir="auto">For larger contributions, consider <a href="/neondatabase/website/blob/main/README.md#getting-started">running the project locally</a> to see how changes look like before making a pull request.</p>
